<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="floatright" style="border:1px solid #AAA; padding: 0px 10px 0px 10px; min-width: 250px;">
<tbody><tr>
<th colspan="2" style="font-size: smaller;"><a href="/wiki/chemical_element" title="chemical element">Chemical element</a>
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: center; font-size: 250%; padding: 0px 10px 5px 0px; vertical-align: middle;"><b>Mg</b>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: left;">Previous: <b><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/sodium#English" title="sodium">sodium</a></span> (Na)</b>

<td>Next: <b><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/aluminium#English" title="aluminium">aluminium</a></span> (Al)</b>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la-new"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Latin">magnēsium</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CE%BC%CE%B1%CE%B3%CE%BD%CE%B7%CF%83%CE%AF%CE%B1#Ancient_Greek" title="μαγνησία">μαγνησία</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">magnēsía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, after <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CE%9C%CE%B1%CE%B3%CE%BD%CE%B7%CF%83%CE%AF%CE%B1#Ancient_Greek" title="Μαγνησία">Μαγνησία</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Magnēsía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="/wiki/Magnesia" title="Magnesia">Magnesia</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a region in Thessaly. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#coinage" title="Appendix:Glossary">Coined</a> by British chemist <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humphry_Davy" class="extiw" title="w:Humphry Davy">Humphry Davy</a>, as a modification of his original suggestion, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/magnium#English" title="magnium">magnium</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">măgnē'zēəm</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˌmæɡˈniːzi.əm/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">măgnē'zēəm</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˌmæɡˈnizi.əm/</span>; <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">măgnē'zhəm</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˌmæɡˈniʒəm/</span></li>
<li><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r50165410">.mw-parser-output .k-player .k-attribution{visibility:hidden}</style><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: middle; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio (US)</td><td class="audiofile"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><span class="mw-tmh-player audio" style="width:175px;"><audio id="mwe_player_0_placeholder" preload="none" width="175" style="width:175px;" data-durationhint="2" data-mwtitle="En-us-magnesium.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" disabled="disabled" tabindex="-1"></audio><a class="mw-tmh-play" href="/wiki/File:En-us-magnesium.ogg" title="Play media" role="button"><span class="mw-tmh-play-icon"></span></a><span class="mw-tmh-duration mw-tmh-label" aria-label="2 seconds">0:02</span></span></span></span></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:En-us-magnesium.ogg" title="File:En-us-magnesium.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li>
<li>Hyphenation: <span class="Latn" lang="en">mag‧ne‧si‧um</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">magnesium</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>)
</p>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/magnesium" class="extiw" title="w:magnesium">magnesium</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/magnesium" class="extiw" title="w:magnesium">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<ol><li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English:_Q660">The <a href="/wiki/chemical_element" title="chemical element">chemical element</a> (<i>symbol</i> Mg) with an <a href="/wiki/atomic_number" title="atomic number">atomic number</a> of 12. It is a <a href="/wiki/light" title="light">light</a>, easily <a href="/wiki/flammable" title="flammable">flammable</a>, <a href="/wiki/silvery-white" title="silvery-white">silvery-white</a> <a href="/wiki/alkaline_earth_metal" title="alkaline earth metal">alkaline earth metal</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1999</b>, Chapter 1 "Barrens" <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Cryptonomicon" class="extiw" title="w:en:Cryptonomicon">Cryptonomicon</a> by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Neal_Stephenson" class="extiw" title="w:en:Neal Stephenson">Neal Stephenson</a>
<dl><dd><i>The building looked only like a wall glowing in the firelight, but sometimes a barrage of <b>magnesium</b> blue light made its windowframes jump out of the darkness.</i></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:CSIRO_ScienceImage_2893_Crystalised_magnesium.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/CSIRO_ScienceImage_2893_Crystalised_magnesium.jpg/220px-CSIRO_ScienceImage_2893_Crystalised_magnesium.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="166" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/CSIRO_ScienceImage_2893_Crystalised_magnesium.jpg/330px-CSIRO_ScienceImage_2893_Crystalised_magnesium.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/CSIRO_ScienceImage_2893_Crystalised_magnesium.jpg/440px-CSIRO_ScienceImage_2893_Crystalised_magnesium.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2296" data-file-height="1728"></a><figcaption>Magnesium sample</figcaption></figure>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Interlingua">Interlingua</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Interlingua">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="ia">magnesium</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">magnesium</a></span></li></ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Latin">Latin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Latin">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_6">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Latin">Classical</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Latin_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Latin pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/maɡˈneː.si.um/</span>, <span class="IPA">[mäŋˈneːs̠iʊ̃ˑ]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ecclesiastical_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Ecclesiastical Latin">Ecclesiastical</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Latin_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Latin pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/maɲˈɲe.si.um/</span>, <span class="IPA">[mäɲˈɲɛːs̬ium]</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/magnesius#Latin" title="magnesius">magnēsius</a></i>.
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la">magnēsium</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/magnesii#Latin" title="magnesii">magnēsiī</a></b>); <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Latin_second_declension" title="Appendix:Latin second declension">second declension</a></i>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="#English">magnesium</a> (chemical element 12)
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1782</b>, D. Laurentius &amp; Gulielmo Huntero, "Nova experimenta Chemica quae ad penitiorem Acidi e Pinguedine eruti cognitionem valere videntur", <i>Philosophical Transactions of the Royal Society of London</i>, Part I, page 28
<dl><dd><i><b>Magnesium</b></i> nitratum nullum converſionem expertum eſt a noſtri acidi admixtione.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=magnesium&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">magnesium</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la-new"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Latin">magnēsium</a></i>.
</p>
